<Rating>4</Rating><review>Perfect place, perfect ambience! I visited this library a few months back and I was very much impressed with its location, lighting, pleasing atmosphere, available topics and arrangement of books, ease of location and access, nice seating, all make it a beautiful library that you feel you should visit often. The registration is very simple and immediate that you can start borrowing number of books and videos at once. You have books on all topics, say, Fiction, non- Fiction, technical, political, educational and so on. You can browse through monitors and make a choice on author or title. This is a free library.
I was surprised to see that there are books on Indian languages like Tamil too.
You have video section too serving movie buffs and others. Number of DVDs and Blu-ray  movies, starting from age old 60's to modern day wait for you to grab. They have latest too. I was delightd to see some old movies too in their collection. There are interesting topics on non-fiction too.
You have facilities for copying, reading leisurely, self ticketing to borrow etc. Rest rooms are good. Parking is very nearby.
The staff are friendly and helpful. You can extend the books on line if required.
This library has kid section too, which is a plus point. While the reading habits are slowly coming down, the introduction of books to children  at an early age is a must to search and gain knowledge instead of digital hunting, Copy-Paste attitude.
Another thing I should mention is the beautiful architecture of the building. Lovely and invites you to visit.
The authorities should be appreciated for all their efforts in maintaining this treasure house of books in excellent condition. Hats off to them!
A place you must visit .< /review>< Pics>

< Review>
The facilities are great and the desks, computers are all new. But in my personal view, a library should be a place where people can read, study, or do other academic work in peace.

However, it is TOTALLY the opposite here. It is so loud. Children run around, occasionally shouting, and parents seems to think that is totally okay. This place is more a day care than a library.

I wish the staff could advise the parents more heavily to remind their children that they are in a library, not a playground.</Review>

< Review>
Great. The place where I love to go every time I can.

There are lot of things anyone can appreciate about library.
Its location is just perfect. Located in river mark market place. You can get almost everything here. Even you might seeking for hair saloon or dentist or cuisine or Safeway or what. Behind library there is big playground too. Parking near library is plus point.
Available facilities are so high that you will overwhelm with those. One day I was asking for librarians that how much books I can take at a time. I was shocked with answer and ask her again. I was not able to believe on my ears. She said 60.
You can renew any book online. There is online catalog available too. Plus anybody can request to HOLD book. Even you can check availability of book. It will give you name of the branch where book is. Reminder for book renewal from library. 2-3 days before. There are always lot of social events going on in library. One can register for it online.
My most favourite part, why I go library every time is for kids. Yes. There is seperate area for kids. Lot of books for toddlers too. Almost on every friday they have story time at 10.30am. Family story time. If its not,  they will update on events calendar. There are many events organised by library for different age groups of kids and adults too. Story time is the best time. My daughter and I both love it.
About the architecture and all it is just perfect. Areas are segregated as per adult and children. Fiction and nonfiction etc. Water fountain, washrooms eveything is available. Copy machine too. Self check out is also there. Many computers provide express check out. Charging point on every table. Group study rooms are there. You can book. One can use library screen for work or search purpose. Behind main library there is some open space. Where you can park  stroller and rest on benches over there.
There are lot of positive thing one must share about this library.  I must say thank you to all  librarians who help me everytime I go there, in everything I need.</Review>

<UserId.>108375423594010502389< /UserId.><Name>Paul Jason<//Name><Date>1484374383297< /Date>< rating>

< Text>
Please increase hours at a few libraries, have a few 24 hr libraries or open very early rather than having so many fancy smhancy branches. Public libraries are the last place where people with no/few resources can gain the knowledge and skills to compete with people with much higher resources. Investment in public libraries have way more multiplier effects and lead to social mobility than investment in roads and fancy buildings. This is especially true in Silicon Valley where the high cost of living keeps people with low resources out. Incumbents will always try to increase the barrier to entry and to create monopolies, and it will protect their interests in the short term. However in the long term, these incumbents who try to build barriers to entry will drive the innovators away to Texas or Boston with much lower cost of living, leading to lower innovation and SV will die a slow death. You as public libraries have this opportunity to lower the barrier to entry and drive innovation and growth in SV more than any other entity, if you chose to take on this role.</Text>

<username>Sherry Campbell<//username><date>1527784078772</date></record></dataset><record>
<rating>5< /rating>< time>
1549678086043<//time>
< Review>
The best coffee around this area, this what Virgil Village used to feel like, from the moment I walked in I could feel the good energy pouring into my soul.

The place is spacious  and is about 3 blocks from Squrl and 1 block west of the fault line. The people who work here are welcoming without being overbearing.

There are vegan options.

There is lots of  parking on Melrose Ave. and some metered parking on Heliotrope.

It is also easily accessible if you are using  the Los Angeles Metro, system, one could easily come here for coffee and take the Melrose bus down to West Hollywood. For those of you who are using AirBnb to stay in East Hollywood, Silver Lake or Los Feliz you can start here and make your way west towards Beverly Hills or East to Downtown Los Angeles or north to the Griffith Park Observatory. The Los Angeles Metro Subway station is 2 blocks north. Easy access to the DASH. A good tip when traveling using the Metro is to buy the day pass for $7.00 which allows the rider to ride all day.

If you are looking for great coffee in the beating heart of Virgil Village in Los Angeles, this is the place you must try.< /Review>

< text>
We were seated instantly. Got here at around 9am for breakfast. Our orders for drinks and food were taken almost as soon as we had decided. Food came in about 8min (yes I time those things) excellent. I had a machaca with eggs, rice & beans plate. It was perfect. After we had finished I forgot I had ordered flan. Asked for it and in a literal minute it was on my table. I cannot express how perfect the consistency of the flan was. I am a stickler for flan, too soft...you might as well call it a custard, too thick...you might as well call it a cake. I have no idea how people can fail at this but Mar y Tierra doesn't. Props.< /text>

My family and I love this place. The owners, Theresa and her chef husband, are awesome. Theresa hand rolls the won tons for their soup daily and everything is so fresh. If you have a favorite Asian dish and it's not on the menu, ask them!  99% of the time they will make it for you.

I'm was very excited to see that they are still open, especially during these hard times. I'm happy to drive out of the way to support this local business. Great location, friendly owners that know your name and what you want to order as soon as they see you walk in, and of course delicious food.< /Text>

<user_id>118109313137905834936< /user_id>< review>
Centrally located in downtown Martinez, the Canton Restaurant is quiet, cozy and the food and service is spot on. Food portions were generous. We visited on 10/15/19 and had the lunchtime specials. I had the Cashew Chicken and my guest had the Sweet and Sour Pork. My guest and I both commented on how savory the soup was. I was expecting the traditional tofu hot/sour soup; however the soup we were served was a bit different. It had small chunks of tomatoes in a savory tomato based stock along with small chunks of tofu and bean sprouts. It was very delicious and took the chill off the cool autumn afternoon. We both chose the pork chow mein instead of the fried rice.  The accompanying spring roll was perfectly crisp and fresh (but it would have been nice to have some sweet sour sauce to dip it in).  There was an abundance of cashews in the Cashew Chicken and the zucchini and sugar snap peas were fresh and crisp, not at all overcooked. We also had a pot of hot tea.

I recommend this restaurant for its food, service and ambience. My only regret is that we didn't sit in the window seat overlooking the street.</review>

< text>
I rode my motorcycle to Martinez recently on a random to see where the front wheel took me.

Finding myself starving and many businesses closed due to C19, I figured I would go back to Pleasant Hill where I started and go to Wendy's.

Canton in downtown MZ was open and I walked in and ordered Mongolian chicken to go (obv).  I got a small order of rice with it and walked out and ate the whole thing on the seat of my bike - using it as a makeshift table.

It was delicious and I didn't ride off needing more food.  $13 bucks very well spent.  I walked back in to thank the owners for taking the chance of being open.

Good ppl.  Give them a try.  BTW, piles of meat in my box.  Not the usu move of a few pieces of meat mixed into a farm of onions and bell peppers and what not.

I will be back!  Next time I will take a pic of the food and post.</text>

<UserId.>111606095798917322219</UserId.><name>Delmy Perez</name><date>1575841215245< /date><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
It was my first time here and I came because of the wide selection of vegan options that they offer. So since I did mot know what I wanted (I recently switched to a vegan diet and was never a big fan of Indian food) I orderes the buffet (since 4 of the options were vegan) and I ordered a mulligatawney soup off the menu.  Everything was so good.  I asked for some extra spice for the soup and they briup me this green chili puree that I added to the soup and it just set off all of the flavors.  I even took a soup to go. The spinach saag was another eye opener.  I never knew steamed spinach could taste so good.  I mixed the saag with some lentil, veggie rice and lime and that green sauce and it was heavenly.  Let me tell you, my eyes are wide open now and I can't beliwvw I have been missing out on Indian food my whole life! The server was excellent! He took the time to point out all pf the vegan options from the buffet and which dressing was vegan as well for my salad.  The menu has a whole page of vegan options, most are also gluten free! Love this place.  So happy I wandered in.< /review>

<Text>Flavor of India is conveniently located in Downtown Burbank. I've never been a fan of Indian food, but since it's been years since I last tried it, I decided to give it a go.

Surprise! Palate was very happy this go around. The garlic naan was incredible. Tandoori chicken was a bit dry, but the sauce was very well done. The butter chicken & tikka masala didn't taste very different to me, but they were both good. The real difference that I could tell was the texture of the sauces. Finally, we also got the vegetable korma, which was my favorite. The food was flavorful and at a good price range, and the service was good. Do keep in mind that I have nothing to compare this experience to, but rather I rate this as an Indian food first timer.

Thank you Flavor of India for awakening my taste buds for Indian food. I'm now aware of a whole cuisine that I have been missing out on.  Great LA local business.<//Text></record></dataset><record>
